                                                                                                                                                                                                                        public class MybatisTest {

    /**
     * åˆ›å»º SqlSessionFactory
     */
    public SqlSessionFactory getSqlSessionFactory() throws IOException {
        return new SqlSessionFactoryBuilder()
            .build(Resources.getResourceAsStream("SqlMapConfig.xml"));
    }
	
    /**
     * åŸºäºæ¥å£ç¼–ç¨‹
     * 1. å‚æ•°ç±»å‹ç”±æ–¹æ³•å‚æ•°ç¡®å®šï¼Œä¸å†æ˜¯ Object
     * 2. ä¸ºæ¥å£åˆ›å»ºä»£ç†å¯¹è±¡ï¼Œç”±ä»£ç†å¯¹è±¡æ‰§è¡ŒCRUDæ“ä½œ
     * 3. Mapper.xml æ–‡ä»¶ä¸­çš„ namespace ä¸ mapperæ¥å£çš„å…¨é™å®šåç›¸åŒ
     * 4. Mapper æ¥å£æ–¹æ³•åå’Œ Mapper.xml ä¸­å®šä¹‰çš„æ¯ä¸ª statement çš„ id ç›¸åŒ
     * 5. Mapper æ¥å£æ–¹æ³•çš„è¾“å…¥å‚æ•°ç±»å‹å’Œ mapper.xmlä¸­å®šä¹‰çš„æ¯ä¸ª sql çš„ parameterType çš„ç±»å‹ç›¸åŒ
     * 6. Mapper æ¥å£æ–¹æ³•çš„è¾“å‡ºå‚æ•°ç±»å‹å’Œ mapper.xmlä¸­å®šä¹‰çš„æ¯ä¸ª sql çš„ resultType çš„ç±»å‹ç›¸åŒ
     */
    @Test
    public void testMybatisGettingStarted() throws IOException {
        SqlSessionFactory sqlSessionFactory = getSqlSessionFactory();
        SqlSession sqlSession = sqlSessionFactory.openSession();
        EmployeeMapper mapper = sqlSession.getMapper(EmployeeMapper.class);
        System.out.println(mapper.getClass());
        // class com.sun.proxy.$Proxy6
        Employee employee = mapper.selectEmployeeById(1);
        System.out.println(employee);
        sqlSession.close();
    }
}

                                                                                                                                                                                                                        Mapper æ¥å£å¼€å‘éœ€è¦éµå¾ªä»¥ä¸‹è§„èŒƒï¼š

                                                                                                                                                                                                                        public interface EmployeeMapper {
     @Select(
         "select id, last_name lastName, email, gender from tbl_employee where id = #{id} "

     public Employee selectEmployeeById(Integer id);

                                                                                                                                                                                                                        SqlSessionFactory build(InputStream inputStream)

                                                                                                                                                                                                                        é€šè¿‡åŠ è½½ Mybatis çš„æ ¸å¿ƒæ–‡ä»¶çš„è¾“å…¥æµçš„å½¢å¼æ„å»º SqlSessionFactory å¯¹è±¡ã€‚å…¶ä¸­ï¼ŒResources å·¥å…·ç±»ï¼Œè¿™ä¸ªç±»åœ¨

                                                                                                                                                                                                                        org.apache.ibatis.ioopen in new window åŒ…ä¸­ã€‚Resources ç±»å¯ä»¥ä»ç±»è·¯å¾„ä¸‹ã€æ–‡ä»¶ç³»ç»Ÿæˆ–ä¸€ä¸ª Web URL ä¸­åŠ è½½èµ„æºæ–‡ä»¶ã€‚

                                                                                                                                                                                                                        InputStream inputStream = Resources.getResourceAsStream("SqlMapConfig.xml");
//åŠ è½½Mybatisé…ç½®æ–‡ä»¶
//InputStream inputStream = getResourceAsStream("SqlMapConfig.xml");
//åˆ›å»ºSqlSessionå·¥å‚
SqlSessionFactoryBuilder sqlSessionFactoryBuilder = new SqlSessionFactoryBuilder();
SqlSessionFactory sqlSessionFactory = sqlSessionFactoryBuilder.build(inputStream);

                                                                                                                                                                                                                        # SqlSessionFactory

                                                                                                                                                                                                                        SqlSessionFactoryï¼šSqlSession å·¥å‚å¯¹è±¡

                                                                                                                                                                                                                        openSession()é»˜è®¤å¼€å¯äº‹ç‰©ï¼Œä½†ä¸ä¼šè‡ªåŠ¨æäº¤

                                                                                                                                                                                                                        # SqlSession

                                                                                                                                                                                                                        ä¼šè¯å¯¹è±¡æ¥å£ï¼Œæ‰§è¡Œè¯­å¥çš„æ–¹æ³•ä¸»è¦æœ‰ï¼š

                                                                                                                                                                                                                        public interface SqlSession extends Closeable {

  /**
   * Retrieve a single row mapped from the statement key.
   * @param <T> the returned object type
   * @param statement
   *          the statement
   * @return Mapped object
   */
  <T> T selectOne(String statement);

  /**
   * Retrieve a single row mapped from the statement key and parameter.
   * @param <T> the returned object type
   * @param statement Unique identifier matching the statement to use.
   * @param parameter A parameter object to pass to the statement.
   * @return Mapped object
   */
  <T> T selectOne(String statement, Object parameter);

  /**
   * Retrieve a list of mapped objects from the statement key.
   * @param <E> the returned list element type
   * @param statement Unique identifier matching the statement to use.
   * @return List of mapped object
   */
  <E> List<E> selectList(String statement);

  /**
   * Retrieve a list of mapped objects from the statement key and parameter.
   * @param <E> the returned list element type
   * @param statement Unique identifier matching the statement to use.
   * @param parameter A parameter object to pass to the statement.
   * @return List of mapped object
   */
  <E> List<E> selectList(String statement, Object parameter);

  /**
   * Retrieve a list of mapped objects from the statement key and parameter,
   * within the specified row bounds.
   * @param <E> the returned list element type
   * @param statement Unique identifier matching the statement to use.
   * @param parameter A parameter object to pass to the statement.
   * @param rowBounds  Bounds to limit object retrieval
   * @return List of mapped object
   */
  <E> List<E> selectList(String statement, Object parameter, RowBounds rowBounds);

  /**
   * The selectMap is a special case in that it is designed to convert a list
   * of results into a Map based on one of the properties in the resulting
   * objects.
   * Eg. Return a of Map[Integer,Author] for selectMap("selectAuthors","id")
   * @param <K> the returned Map keys type
   * @param <V> the returned Map values type
   * @param statement Unique identifier matching the statement to use.
   * @param mapKey The property to use as key for each value in the list.
   * @return Map containing key pair data.
   */
  <K, V> Map<K, V> selectMap(String statement, String mapKey);

  /**
   * The selectMap is a special case in that it is designed to convert a list
   * of results into a Map based on one of the properties in the resulting
   * objects.
   * @param <K> the returned Map keys type
   * @param <V> the returned Map values type
   * @param statement Unique identifier matching the statement to use.
   * @param parameter A parameter object to pass to the statement.
   * @param mapKey The property to use as key for each value in the list.
   * @return Map containing key pair data.
   */
  <K, V> Map<K, V> selectMap(String statement, Object parameter, String mapKey);

  /**
   * The selectMap is a special case in that it is designed to convert a list
   * of results into a Map based on one of the properties in the resulting
   * objects.
   * @param <K> the returned Map keys type
   * @param <V> the returned Map values type
   * @param statement Unique identifier matching the statement to use.
   * @param parameter A parameter object to pass to the statement.
   * @param mapKey The property to use as key for each value in the list.
   * @param rowBounds  Bounds to limit object retrieval
   * @return Map containing key pair data.
   */
  <K, V> Map<K, V> selectMap(String statement, Object parameter, String mapKey, RowBounds rowBounds);

  /**
   * A Cursor offers the same results as a List, except it fetches data lazily using an Iterator.
   * @param <T> the returned cursor element type.
   * @param statement Unique identifier matching the statement to use.
   * @return Cursor of mapped objects
   */
  <T> Cursor<T> selectCursor(String statement);

  /**
   * A Cursor offers the same results as a List, except it fetches data lazily using an Iterator.
   * @param <T> the returned cursor element type.
   * @param statement Unique identifier matching the statement to use.
   * @param parameter A parameter object to pass to the statement.
   * @return Cursor of mapped objects
   */
  <T> Cursor<T> selectCursor(String statement, Object parameter);

  /**
   * A Cursor offers the same results as a List, except it fetches data lazily using an Iterator.
   * @param <T> the returned cursor element type.
   * @param statement Unique identifier matching the statement to use.
   * @param parameter A parameter object to pass to the statement.
   * @param rowBounds  Bounds to limit object retrieval
   * @return Cursor of mapped objects
   */
  <T> Cursor<T> selectCursor(String statement, Object parameter, RowBounds rowBounds);

  /**
   * Retrieve a single row mapped from the statement key and parameter
   * using a {@code ResultHandler}.
   * @param statement Unique identifier matching the statement to use.
   * @param parameter A parameter object to pass to the statement.
   * @param handler ResultHandler that will handle each retrieved row
   */
  void select(String statement, Object parameter, ResultHandler handler);

  /**
   * Retrieve a single row mapped from the statement
   * using a {@code ResultHandler}.
   * @param statement Unique identifier matching the statement to use.
   * @param handler ResultHandler that will handle each retrieved row
   */
  void select(String statement, ResultHandler handler);

  /**
   * Retrieve a single row mapped from the statement key and parameter using a {@code ResultHandler} and
   * {@code RowBounds}.
   *
   * @param statement
   *          Unique identifier matching the statement to use.
   * @param parameter
   *          the parameter
   * @param rowBounds
   *          RowBound instance to limit the query results
   * @param handler
   *          ResultHandler that will handle each retrieved row
   */
  void select(String statement, Object parameter, RowBounds rowBounds, ResultHandler handler);

  /**
   * Execute an insert statement.
   * @param statement Unique identifier matching the statement to execute.
   * @return int The number of rows affected by the insert.
   */
  int insert(String statement);

  /**
   * Execute an insert statement with the given parameter object. Any generated
   * autoincrement values or selectKey entries will modify the given parameter
   * object properties. Only the number of rows affected will be returned.
   * @param statement Unique identifier matching the statement to execute.
   * @param parameter A parameter object to pass to the statement.
   * @return int The number of rows affected by the insert.
   */
  int insert(String statement, Object parameter);

  /**
   * Execute an update statement. The number of rows affected will be returned.
   * @param statement Unique identifier matching the statement to execute.
   * @return int The number of rows affected by the update.
   */
  int update(String statement);

  /**
   * Execute an update statement. The number of rows affected will be returned.
   * @param statement Unique identifier matching the statement to execute.
   * @param parameter A parameter object to pass to the statement.
   * @return int The number of rows affected by the update.
   */
  int update(String statement, Object parameter);

  /**
   * Execute a delete statement. The number of rows affected will be returned.
   * @param statement Unique identifier matching the statement to execute.
   * @return int The number of rows affected by the delete.
   */
  int delete(String statement);

  /**
   * Execute a delete statement. The number of rows affected will be returned.
   * @param statement Unique identifier matching the statement to execute.
   * @param parameter A parameter object to pass to the statement.
   * @return int The number of rows affected by the delete.
   */
  int delete(String statement, Object parameter);

  /**
   * Flushes batch statements and commits database connection.
   * Note that database connection will not be committed if no updates/deletes/inserts were called.
   * To force the commit call {@link SqlSession#commit(boolean)}
   */
  void commit();

  /**
   * Flushes batch statements and commits database connection.
   * @param force forces connection commit
   */
  void commit(boolean force);

  /**
   * Discards pending batch statements and rolls database connection back.
   * Note that database connection will not be rolled back if no updates/deletes/inserts were called.
   * To force the rollback call {@link SqlSession#rollback(boolean)}
   */
  void rollback();

  /**
   * Discards pending batch statements and rolls database connection back.
   * Note that database connection will not be rolled back if no updates/deletes/inserts were called.
   * @param force forces connection rollback
   */
  void rollback(boolean force);

  /**
   * Flushes batch statements.
   * @return BatchResult list of updated records
   * @since 3.0.6
   */
  List<BatchResult> flushStatements();

  /**
   * Closes the session.
   */
  @Override
  void close();

  /**
   * Clears local session cache.
   */
  void clearCache();

  /**
   * Retrieves current configuration.
   * @return Configuration
   */
  Configuration getConfiguration();

  /**
   * Retrieves a mapper.
   * @param <T> the mapper type
   * @param type Mapper interface class
   * @return a mapper bound to this SqlSession
   */
  <T> T getMapper(Class<T> type);

  /**
   * Retrieves inner database connection.
   * @return Connection
   */
  Connection getConnection();
}

}

                                                                                                                                                                                                                        Employee

                                                                                                                                                                                                                        @Data
@AllArgsConstructor
@NoArgsConstructor
public class Employee implements Serializable {
    private Integer id;
    private String lastName;
    private String gender;
    private String email;

    private EmployeeStatus status;

    public Employee(String lastName, String gender, String email) {
        this.lastName = lastName;
        this.gender = gender;
        this.email = email;
    }

    public Employee(String lastName, String gender, String email, EmployeeStatus status) {
        this.lastName = lastName;
        this.gender = gender;
        this.email = email;
        this.status = status;
    }
}

                                                                                                                                                                                                                        EmployeeStatus

                                                                                                                                                                                                                        public enum EmployeeStatus {
    LOGIN(100,"ç™»å½•"),LOGOUT(200,"é€€å‡º"),REMOVE(300,"åˆ é™¤");

    private Integer code;
    private String message;

    private EmployeeStatus(Integer code, String message){
        this.code = code;
        this.message = message;
    }
    public static EmployeeStatus getEmpStatusByCode(Integer code) {
        switch (code) {
            case 100:
                return LOGIN;
            case 200:
                return LOGOUT;
            default:
                return REMOVE;
        }
    }
}

                                                                                                                                                                                                                        è‡ªå®šä¹‰ç±»å‹å¤„ç†å™¨

                                                                                                                                                                                                                        package com.example.mybatis.typehandlers;

import com.example.mybatis.bean.EmployeeStatus;
import org.apache.ibatis.type.JdbcType;
import org.apache.ibatis.type.TypeHandler;

import java.sql.CallableStatement;
import java.sql.PreparedStatement;
import java.sql.ResultSet;
import java.sql.SQLException;

/**
 * è‡ªå®šä¹‰ç±»å‹å¤„ç†å™¨
 */
public class EmployeeEnumTypeHandler implements TypeHandler<EmployeeStatus> {

    @Override
    public void setParameter(PreparedStatement ps, int i, EmployeeStatus parameter, JdbcType jdbcType) throws SQLException {
        ps.setString(i, parameter.getCode().toString());
    }

    @Override
    public EmployeeStatus getResult(ResultSet rs, String columnName) throws SQLException {
        return EmployeeStatus.getEmployeeStatusByCode(rs.getInt(columnName));
    }

    @Override
    public EmployeeStatus getResult(ResultSet rs, int columnIndex) throws SQLException {
        return EmployeeStatus.getEmployeeStatusByCode(rs.getInt(columnIndex));
    }

    @Override
    public EmployeeStatus getResult(CallableStatement cs, int columnIndex) throws SQLException {
        return null;
    }
}

                values (#{lastName}, #{gender}, #{email}, #{empStatus,typeHandler=....})

                                                                                                                                                                                                                        EmployeeTypeHandlerMapper.xml

                                                                                                                                                                                                                        <?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8" ?>
<!DOCTYPE mapper
        PUBLIC "-//mybatis.org//DTD Mapper 3.0//EN"
        "http://mybatis.org/dtd/mybatis-3-mapper.dtd">
<mapper namespace="com.example.mybatis.mapper.EmployeeTypeHandlerMapper">

    <resultMap id="BaseResultMap" type="com.example.mybatis.bean.Employee">
        <id column="id" property="id"/>
        <result column="last_name" property="lastName"/>
        <result column="employeeStatus" property="employeeStatus"/>
    </resultMap>

    <insert id="insertEmployee" useGeneratedKeys="true" keyProperty="id">
        insert into tbl_employee(last_name, gender, email, employeeStatus)
        values (#{lastName}, #{gender}, #{email}, #{employeeStatus})
    </insert>

    <select id="selectEmployeeById" resultMap="BaseResultMap">
        select * from tbl_employee where id = #{id}
    </select>

</mapper>

                                                                                                                                                                                                                        æµ‹è¯• MybatisTypeHandlerMapperTestï¼š

                                                                                                                                                                                                                        public class MybatisTypeHandlerMapperTest {
    public SqlSessionFactory getSqlSessionFactory() throws IOException {
        return new SqlSessionFactoryBuilder()
                .build(Resources.getResourceAsStream("mybatis-config.xml"));
    }

    /**
     * è‡ªå®šä¹‰ç±»å‹å¤„ç†å™¨
     */
    @Test
    public void testBatchMapper() throws IOException {
        SqlSessionFactory sqlSessionFactory = getSqlSessionFactory();
        SqlSession sqlSession = sqlSessionFactory.openSession();
        try {
            EmployeeTypeHandlerMapper mapper =
                    sqlSession.getMapper(EmployeeTypeHandlerMapper.class);
            Employee employee = new Employee("enum", "M", "enum@example.com", EmployeeStatus.LOGOUT);
            mapper.insertEmployee(employee);
            System.out.println(employee.getId() + " : " + employee.getEmployeeStatus());
            System.out.println(mapper.selectEmployeeById(16));
            sqlSession.commit();
        } finally {
            sqlSession.close();
        }
    }
}

                                                                                                                                                                                                                        # plugins

                                                                                                                                                                                                                        æ’ä»¶å¼€å‘æ­¥éª¤ï¼š

                                                                                                                                                                                                                        1. ç¼–å†™æ’ä»¶å®ç° Interceptor æ¥å£ï¼Œå¹¶ä½¿ç”¨ @Intercepts æ³¨è§£å®Œæˆæ’ä»¶ç­¾å

                                                                                                                                                                                                                          public interface Interceptor {

  Object intercept(Invocation invocation) throws Throwable;

  default Object plugin(Object target) {
    return Plugin.wrap(target, this);
  }

  default void setProperties(Properties properties) {
    // NOP
  }

}

                                                                                                                                                                                                                        2. åœ¨å…¨å±€é…ç½®æ–‡ä»¶ä¸­æ³¨å†Œæ’ä»¶

    <!--é…ç½®åˆ†é¡µæ’ä»¶ PageHelper-->

    <!--è‡ªå®šä¹‰æ’ä»¶-->

                                                                                                                                                                                                                        åŸºæœ¬ç¤ºä¾‹ï¼š

                                                                                                                                                                                                                        ä¿®æ”¹é¢„ç¼–è¯‘å‚æ•°ï¼Œä¼ å…¥ ID ä¸º 1 çš„æ•°æ®è¿›è¡ŒæŸ¥è¯¢ï¼Œå®é™…æŸ¥è¯¢ ID ä¸º 2 çš„æ•°æ®ã€‚

                                                                                                                                                                                                                        @Intercepts({
        @Signature(type = StatementHandler.class,
                method = "parameterize", args = Statement.class)
})
public class CustomParameterPlugin implements Interceptor {

    /**
     * æ‹¦æˆªç›®æ ‡æ–¹æ³•æ‰§è¡Œ
     */
    @Override
    public Object intercept(Invocation invocation) throws Throwable {
        //æ’ä»¶æ‹¦æˆªçš„æ–¹æ³•
        System.out.println("Custom SecondPlugin intercept: " + invocation.getMethod());
        Object target = invocation.getTarget();
        System.out.println("intercept: " + target);
        //è·å–targetçš„å…ƒæ•°æ®
        MetaObject metaObject = SystemMetaObject.forObject(target);
        Object objectValue = metaObject.getValue("parameterHandler.parameterObject");
        System.out.println("é¢„ç¼–è¯‘å‚æ•°ï¼š" + objectValue);
        //ä¿®æ”¹å‚æ•°
        metaObject.setValue("parameterHandler.parameterObject",2);
        //æ‰§è¡Œç›®æ ‡æ–¹æ³•
        Object proceed = invocation.proceed();
        return proceed;
    }

    /**
     * ç”ŸæˆåŠ¨æ€ä»£ç†å¯¹è±¡ï¼Œå¯ä»¥ä½¿ç”¨ MyBatis æ
     * ä¾›çš„ Plugin ç±»çš„ wrapæ–¹æ³•
     */
    @Override
    public Object plugin(Object target) {
        /*
            æ’ä»¶åŒ…è£…çš„æ–¹æ³•ï¼Œtargetï¼šè¦åŒ…è£…çš„å¯¹è±¡
         */
        System.out.println("Custom SecondPlugin plugin: " + target);
        //Mybatisæä¾›äº†Plugin.wrapä½¿ç”¨å½“å‰æ‹¦æˆªå™¨åŒ…è£…ç›®æ ‡æ–¹æ³•ï¼Œè¿”å›åŒ…è£…åçš„å¯¹è±¡
        Object wrap = Plugin.wrap(target, this);
        return wrap;
    }

    /**
     * æ³¨å…¥æ’ä»¶é…ç½®æ—¶è®¾ç½®çš„å±æ€§
     */
    @Override
    public void setProperties(Properties properties) {
        //Interceptor.super.setProperties(properties);
        System.out.println(properties);
    }
}

                                                                                                                                                                                                                        å…¨å±€é…ç½®ï¼š

    <plugin interceptor="com.example.mybatis.plugin.CustomParameterPlugin"/>
</plugins>

                                                                                                                                                                                                                        æµ‹è¯•è‡ªå®šä¹‰æ’ä»¶

                                                                                                                                                                                                                            /**
     * æµ‹è¯•è‡ªå®šä¹‰æ’ä»¶
     */
    @Test
    public void testCustomPlugin() throws IOException {
        try (SqlSession sqlSession = getSqlSessionFactory().openSession()) {
            EmployeePluginMapper mapper = sqlSession.getMapper(EmployeePluginMapper.class);
            Employee employeeById = mapper.selectEmployeeById(1);
            System.out.println(employeeById);
        }
    }

                                                                                                                                                                                                                        ä¿®æ”¹ POJOï¼š

                                                                                                                                                                                                                        @Data
@AllArgsConstructor
@NoArgsConstructor
//@Alias(value = "emp")
public class Employee {
    private Integer id;
    private String lastName;
    private String gender;
    private String email;
    private String employeeStatus;
    private Integer deptId;
    private Department department;

    
    public Employee(Integer id, String lastName, String gender, String email) {
        this.id = id;
        this.lastName = lastName;
        this.gender = gender;
        this.email = email;
    }

    public Employee(String lastName, String gender, String email, 
                    String employeeStatus, Integer deptId) {
        this.lastName = lastName;
        this.gender = gender;
        this.email = email;
        this.employeeStatus = employeeStatus;
        this.deptId = deptId;
    }

}

                                                                                                                                                                                                                        @Data
@AllArgsConstructor
@NoArgsConstructor
public class Department {
    private Integer id;
    private String departmentName;
    private List<Employee> employeeList;
}

                                                                                                                                                                                                                        /**
 * Mybatis CRUD
 */
public interface EmployeeCRUDMapper {
    /**
     * æ ¹æ® id æŸ¥è¯¢
     */
    public Employee selectEmployeeById(Integer id);

    /**
     * æ–°å¢
     */
    public void insertEmployee(Employee employee);

    /**
     * æ–°å¢è¿”å›ä¸»é”®
     */
    public Integer insertEmployeeGetGeneratedKey(Employee employee);

    /**
     * ä¿®æ”¹
     */
    public void updateEmployeeById(Employee employee);

    /**
     * åˆ é™¤å•ä¸ª
     */
    public void deleteEmployeeById(Integer id);
}

    <select id="selectEmployeeById" resultType="employee" databaseId="mysql">
        SELECT
            *
        FROM
            tbl_employee
        WHERE
            id = #{id}
    </select>

    <select id="selectEmployeeById" resultType="employee" databaseId="oracle">
        SELECT
            empno id,
            ename lastName
        FROM
            emp
        WHERE
            empno = #{id}
    </select>

    <!--
        parameterTypeï¼šå‚æ•°ç±»å‹ï¼Œå¯ä»¥çœç•¥(Mybatisä¼šè‡ªåŠ¨æ ¹æ®ç±»å‹æ¨æ–­)
    -->
    <insert id="insertEmployee">
        INSERT INTO tbl_employee ( last_name, gender, email )
        VALUES
            (#{lastName}, #{gender}, #{email})
    </insert>

    <update id="updateEmployeeById">
        UPDATE tbl_employee
        SET last_name = #{lastName},
            gender = #{gender},
            email = #{email}
        WHERE
            id = #{id}SELECT * FROM tbl_employee
    </update>

    <delete id="deleteEmployeeById">
        DELETE
        FROM
            tbl_employee
        WHERE
            id = #{id}
    </delete>
</mapper>

                                                                                                                                                                                                                        æµ‹è¯•ï¼š

                                                                                                                                                                                                                        /**
 * æµ‹è¯•CRUD
 */
public class MybatisCRUDMapperTest {

    public SqlSessionFactory getSqlSessionFactory() {
        try {
            return new SqlSessionFactoryBuilder().build(Resources.getResourceAsStream("mybatis-config.xml"));
        } catch (IOException e) {
            throw new RuntimeException(e);
        }
    }

    /**
     * æµ‹è¯• CRUD
     */
    @Test
    public void testCRUD() {
        SqlSessionFactory sqlSessionFactory = getSqlSessionFactory();
        /*
            openSession(): é»˜è®¤ä¸º falseï¼Œå¯¹äºæ–°å¢ä¿®æ”¹åˆ é™¤ä¸ä¼šè‡ªåŠ¨æäº¤ï¼Œéœ€è¦æ‰‹åŠ¨ sqlSession.commit();
            è®¾ç½®ä¸º true æ—¶ï¼Œè‡ªåŠ¨æäº¤
         */
        try (SqlSession sqlSession = sqlSessionFactory.openSession()) {
            EmployeeCRUDMapper mapper = sqlSession.getMapper(EmployeeCRUDMapper.class);
            Employee employee = new Employee(
                    "MineTing", "M", "mineting@example.com", "200", 2);
            mapper.insertEmployee(employee);
            employee.setId(2);
            employee.setLastName(employee.getLastName() + " : Fei");
            mapper.updateEmployeeById(employee);
            //mapper.deleteEmployeeById(1);
            Employee employeeById = mapper.selectEmployeeById(2);
            System.out.println(employeeById);
            sqlSession.commit();
        }
    }

    /**
     * æµ‹è¯•æ’å…¥è¿”å›ä¸»é”®å€¼
     */
    @Test
    public void testGeneratedKey() {
        try (SqlSession sqlSession = getSqlSessionFactory().openSession(true)) {
            EmployeeCRUDMapper mapper = sqlSession.getMapper(EmployeeCRUDMapper.class);
            Employee employee = new Employee(
                    "MineTing", "M", "mineting@example.com", "200", 2);
            Integer rows = mapper.insertEmployeeGetGeneratedKey(employee);
            Integer insertId = employee.getId();
            System.out.println("rows: " + rows + ", insertId: " + insertId);
        }
    }
}

                                                                                                                                                                                                                        # Mybatis å‚æ•°å¤„ç†æºç 

                                                                                                                                                                                                                        æ—¶åºå›¾ï¼šï¼ˆç•¥ï¼‰

                                                                                                                                                                                                                        åˆ©ç”¨åå°„ï¼šMapperMethodInvoker

                                                                                                                                                                                                                        @Override
public Object invoke(Object proxy, Method method, Object[] args, SqlSession sqlSession) throws Throwable {
    return mapperMethod.execute(sqlSession, args);
}

                                                                                                                                                                                                                          public Object execute(SqlSession sqlSession, Object[] args) {
    Object result;
    switch (command.getType()) {
      case INSERT: {
        Object param = method.convertArgsToSqlCommandParam(args);
        result = rowCountResult(sqlSession.insert(command.getName(), param));
        break;
      }
      case UPDATE: {
        Object param = method.convertArgsToSqlCommandParam(args);
        result = rowCountResult(sqlSession.update(command.getName(), param));
        break;
      }
      case DELETE: {
        Object param = method.convertArgsToSqlCommandParam(args);
        result = rowCountResult(sqlSession.delete(command.getName(), param));
        break;
      }
      case SELECT:
        if (method.returnsVoid() && method.hasResultHandler()) {
          executeWithResultHandler(sqlSession, args);
          result = null;
        } else if (method.returnsMany()) {
          result = executeForMany(sqlSession, args);
        } else if (method.returnsMap()) {
          result = executeForMap(sqlSession, args);
        } else if (method.returnsCursor()) {
          result = executeForCursor(sqlSession, args);
        } else {
          Object param = method.convertArgsToSqlCommandParam(args);
          result = sqlSession.selectOne(command.getName(), param);
          if (method.returnsOptional()
              && (result == null || !method.getReturnType().equals(result.getClass()))) {
            result = Optional.ofNullable(result);
          }
        }
        break;
      case FLUSH:
        result = sqlSession.flushStatements();
        break;
      default:
        throw new BindingException("Unknown execution method for: " + command.getName());
    }
    if (result == null && method.getReturnType().isPrimitive() && !method.returnsVoid()) {
      throw new BindingException("Mapper method '" + command.getName()
          + " attempted to return null from a method with a primitive return type (" + method.getReturnType() + ").");
    }
    return result;
  }


                                                                                                                                                                                                                          private <E> Object executeForMany(SqlSession sqlSession, Object[] args) {
    List<E> result;
    Object param = method.convertArgsToSqlCommandParam(args);
    if (method.hasRowBounds()) {
      RowBounds rowBounds = method.extractRowBounds(args);
      result = sqlSession.selectList(command.getName(), param, rowBounds);
    } else {
      result = sqlSession.selectList(command.getName(), param);
    }
    // issue #510 Collections & arrays support
    if (!method.getReturnType().isAssignableFrom(result.getClass())) {
      if (method.getReturnType().isArray()) {
        return convertToArray(result);
      } else {
        return convertToDeclaredCollection(sqlSession.getConfiguration(), result);
      }
    }
    return result;
  }


                                                                                                                                                                                                                            public Object convertArgsToSqlCommandParam(Object[] args) {
      return paramNameResolver.getNamedParams(args);
    }

                                                                                                                                                                                                                          public Object getNamedParams(Object[] args) {
    final int paramCount = names.size();
    if (args == null || paramCount == 0) {
      return null;
    } else if (!hasParamAnnotation && paramCount == 1) {
      Object value = args[names.firstKey()];
      return wrapToMapIfCollection(value, useActualParamName ? names.get(0) : null);
    } else {
      final Map<String, Object> param = new ParamMap<>();
      int i = 0;
      for (Map.Entry<Integer, String> entry : names.entrySet()) {
        param.put(entry.getValue(), args[entry.getKey()]);
        // add generic param names (param1, param2, ...)
        final String genericParamName = GENERIC_NAME_PREFIX + (i + 1);
        // ensure not to overwrite parameter named with @Param
        if (!names.containsValue(genericParamName)) {
          param.put(genericParamName, args[entry.getKey()]);
        }
        i++;
      }
      return param;
    }
  }

            *
        FROM
            tbl_employee
        WHERE
            last_name LIKE concat('%',#{lastName},'%')
    </select>
</mapper>

                                                                                                                                                                                                                        Employee

                                                                                                                                                                                                                        @Data
@AllArgsConstructor
@NoArgsConstructor
//@Alias(value = "emp")
public class Employee {
    private Integer id;
    private String lastName;
    private String gender;
    private String email;
    private String employeeStatus;
    private Integer deptId;
    private Department department;

    public Employee(Integer id, String lastName, String gender, String email) {
        this.id = id;
        this.lastName = lastName;
        this.gender = gender;
        this.email = email;
    }

    public Employee(String lastName, String gender, String email, String employeeStatus, Integer deptId) {
        this.lastName = lastName;
        this.gender = gender;
        this.email = email;
        this.employeeStatus = employeeStatus;
        this.deptId = deptId;
    }

}

        <result column="did" property="department.id"/>
        <result column="dept_name" property="department.departmentName"/>
    </resultMap>

        å…³è”æŸ¥è¯¢äºŒï¼šä½¿ç”¨associationå®šä¹‰å•ä¸ªå¯¹è±¡çš„å°è£…è§„åˆ™

            <!--æ­¤å¤„ä¸èƒ½å’Œemployeeçš„idç›¸åŒ-->
            <id column="did" property="id"/>
            <result column="dept_name" property="departmentName"/>
        </association>
    </resultMap>

    <select id="selectEmployeeAndDepartmentById" resultMap="employeeMap">
        SELECT
            e.id id,
            e.last_name,
            e.email,
            e.gender,
            d.id did,
            d.dept_name
        FROM
            tbl_employee e,
            tbl_dept d
        WHERE
            e.dept_id = d.id
          AND e.id = #{id}
    </select>
</mapper>

                                                                                                                                                                                                                        /**
 * æµ‹è¯•è‡ªåŠ¨æ˜ å°„
 */
public class MybatisResultMapTest {
    /**
     * æ³¨æ„SqlSessionä¸æ˜¯çº¿ç¨‹å®‰å…¨çš„ï¼Œä¸èƒ½å®šä¹‰ä¸ºå…¨éƒ¨å˜é‡ï¼Œä½¿ç”¨ååº”è¯¥åŠæ—¶å…³é—­
     * private SqlSession sqlSession;
     */
    public SqlSessionFactory getSqlSessionFactory() throws IOException {
        return new SqlSessionFactoryBuilder()
            .build(Resources.getResourceAsStream("mybatis-config.xml"));
    }

    @Test
    public void testResultMap01() throws IOException {
        SqlSession sqlSession = getSqlSessionFactory().openSession();
        EmployeeResultMapMapper mapper = sqlSession.getMapper(EmployeeResultMapMapper.class);
        // Employee employee = mapper.selectEmployeeById(1);
        Employee employee = mapper.selectEmployeeAndDepartmentById(1);
        // Employee employee = mapper.selectEmployeeByStep(1);
        // System.out.println("lazyTest: " + employee.getLastName());
        // å»¶è¿ŸåŠ è½½
        // System.out.println(employee.getDepartment());
        System.out.println(employee);
        sqlSession.close();
    }
}

        "http://mybatis.org/dtd/mybatis-3-mapper.dtd">
<mapper namespace="com.example.mybatis.mapper.DepartmentMapper">

    <resultMap id="baseMap" type="department">
        <id column="id" property="id"/>
        <result column="dept_name" property="departmentName"/>
    </resultMap>

    <select id="selectDepartmentById" resultMap="baseMap">
        SELECT
            *
        FROM
            tbl_dept
        WHERE
            id = #{id}
    </select>

    <!--
        å…³è”æŸ¥è¯¢å››ï¼šcollection
    -->
    <resultMap id="collectionMap" type="department">
        <id column="did" property="id"/>
        <result column="department_name" property="departmentName"/>
        <!--
            collectionï¼šå®šä¹‰å…³è”é›†åˆçš„å°è£…è§„åˆ™
                ofTypeï¼šé›†åˆä¸­å…ƒç´ ç±»å‹ï¼Œå¯çœç•¥
        -->
        <collection property="employeeList" ofType="employee">
            <id column="id" property="id"/>
            <result column="last_name" property="lastName"/>
            <result column="email" property="email"/>
            <result column="gender" property="gender"/>
        </collection>
    </resultMap>


    <select id="selectDepartmentAndEmployeeById" resultMap="collectionMap">
        SELECT
            d.id did,
            d.department_name dept_name,
            e.id id,
            e.last_name last_name,
            e.email email,
            e.gender gender
        FROM
            tbl_dept d
                LEFT JOIN tbl_employee e ON d.id = e.d_id
        WHERE
            d.id = #{id}
    </select>

    <!--
        å…³è”æŸ¥è¯¢å››ï¼šcollectionåˆ†æ­¥æŸ¥è¯¢
    -->
    <resultMap id="collectionMapStep" type="department">
        <id column="id" property="id"/>
        <result column="department_name" property="departmentName"/>
        <!--<collection property="employeeList"
                    select="com.example.mybatis.mapper.EmployeeResultMapMapper.selectEmployeeByDeptId"
                    column="id"/>-->
        <!--
            ä¼ é€’å¤šåˆ—çš„å€¼ï¼šå°è£…ä¸ºmapä¼ é€’
            column={key1=column1,key2=column2}
            æ³¨æ„ï¼šé”®å¿…é¡»ç›¸åŒ

            fetchTypeï¼šå…¨å±€å»¶è¿ŸåŠ è½½ï¼Œè¯¥å±æ€§æŒ‡å®šå±€éƒ¨åŠ è½½æ–¹å¼ï¼š
                eagerï¼šç«‹å³åŠ è½½
                lazyï¼šå»¶è¿ŸåŠ è½½
        -->
        <collection property="employeeList"
                    select="com.example.mybatis.mapper.EmployeeResultMapMapper.selectEmployeeByDeptId"
                    column="{deptId=id}" fetchType="eager"/>
    </resultMap>

    <select id="selectDepartmentAndEmployeeByStep" resultMap="collectionMapStep">
        SELECT
            *
        FROM
            tbl_dept
        WHERE
            id = #{id}
    </select>
</mapper>

                                                                                                                                                                                                                        # åˆ†æ­¥æŸ¥è¯¢

                                                                                                                                                                                                                        åˆ†å¸ƒæŸ¥è¯¢ä¸€èˆ¬æ­é…å»¶è¿ŸåŠ è½½ä½¿ç”¨ï¼Œä¼šå‘é€å¤šæ¡ SQL è¯­å¥

                                                                                                                                                                                                                        <!--
    å…³è”æŸ¥è¯¢ä¸‰ï¼šåˆ†æ­¥æŸ¥è¯¢
    å…ˆæ ¹æ® employee çš„ id æŸ¥å‡ºä¿¡æ¯ï¼Œå†æ ¹æ® dept_id åœ¨ DepartmentMapper ä¸­æŸ¥å‡º dept ä¿¡æ¯
    SQLè¯­å¥ä¼šåˆ†æ­¥ï¼š
        Preparing: select * from tbl_employee where id = ?
        Parameters: 1(Integer)
        Preparing: select * from tbl_dept where id = ?
        Parameters: 1(Integer)

<resultMap id="byStepMap" type="employee" autoMapping="true">
    <id column="id" property="id"/>
    <result column="last_name" property="lastName"/>
    <!--
        associationåˆ†æ­¥æŸ¥è¯¢ï¼š
        selectï¼šè¡¨ç¤ºå½“å‰å±æ€§æ—¶è°ƒç”¨selectæ–¹æ³•æŸ¥å‡ºçš„ç»“æœ
        columnï¼šæŒ‡å®šå°†é‚£ä¸€åˆ—çš„å€¼ä¼ é€’ç»™è¯¥æ–¹æ³•
                ä¼ é€’å•åˆ—çš„å€¼ï¼šç›´æ¥ä½¿ç”¨åˆ—åå³å¯
                ä¼ é€’å¤šåˆ—çš„å€¼ï¼š{key1=column1,key2=column2}
							å¦‚{id=dept_id}
    -->
    <association property="department"
                 select="com.example.mybatis.mapper.DepartmentMapper.selectDepartmentById"
                 column="dept_id"/>
</resultMap>

<mapper namespace="com.example.mybatis.mapper.EmployeeDynamicSqlMapper">
    <!--
        ifæ ‡ç­¾ï¼štestæ¡ä»¶
        ç‰¹æ®Šç¬¦å·ä½¿ç”¨ï¼šå¦‚åŒå¼•å· &quot;  &&(and) &amp;&amp;
        å¦‚æœéƒ¨åˆ†æ¡ä»¶ä¸æ»¡è¶³ï¼Œä¼šé€ æˆSQLé”™è¯¯ï¼Œè§£å†³æ–¹æ³•ï¼š
            1. where 1=1 and ...
            2. ä½¿ç”¨<where>æ ‡ç­¾å¯ä»¥å»æ‰â€œè¯­å¥å‰çš„and/orâ€,ä½†ä¸èƒ½å»æ‰â€œè¯­å¥åçš„and/orâ€

    <select id="selectEmployeeByConditionIf" resultType="employee">
        select * from tbl_employee
        <where>
            <if test="id!=null">
                id = #{id}
            </if>
            <!--<if test="lastName!=null &amp;&amp; lastName!=&quot;&quot;">-->
            <if test="lastName!=null and lastName!=''">
                and last_name like #{lastName}
            </if>
            <if test="gender==0 or gender==1">
                and gender = #{gender}
            </if>
            <if test="email!=null and email.trim()!=''">
                and email =#{email}
            </if>
        </where>
    </select>
</mapper>

                                                                                                                                                                                                                        public class MybatisDynamicSqlMapperTest {

        List<Employee> employeeList = mapper.selectEmployeeByConditionIf(employee);
    }

                                                                                                                                                                                                                            <!--
        chooseï¼š
            åªä¼šè¿›å…¥ä¸€ä¸ªåˆ†æ”¯ï¼Œç±»ä¼¼äºswitch-case
            whenï¼šæ¡ä»¶
            otherwiseï¼šéƒ½ä¸æ»¡è¶³
    -->

                <when test="lastName!=null">

                </when>
                <when test="email!=null">
                    email=#{email}
                </when>
                <otherwise>
                    1=1
                </otherwise>
            </choose>
        </where>
    </select>

                                                                                                                                                                                                                        æµ‹è¯•ï¼š

                                                                                                                                                                                                                        /**
 * æµ‹è¯•æ‰¹é‡ä¿å­˜
 */
@Test
public void testBatchInsert() throws IOException {
    SqlSession sqlSession = getSqlSessionFactory().openSession(true);
    EmployeeDynamicSqlMapper mapper = sqlSession.getMapper(EmployeeDynamicSqlMapper.class);
    List<Employee> employeeList = new ArrayList<>();
    employeeList.add(new Employee(null, "E-001", null, null));
    employeeList.add(new Employee(null, "E-002", null, null));
    mapper.insertEmployeeBatch(employeeList);
    sqlSession.close();
}

    /**
     * ä¸€çº§ç¼“å­˜
     * 1. sqlSessionçº§åˆ«çš„ç¼“å­˜,ä¸€çº§ç¼“å­˜æ˜¯ä¸€ç›´å¼€å¯çš„ï¼›SqlSessionçº§åˆ«çš„ä¸€ä¸ªMap,
	 *    key : hashCode + æŸ¥è¯¢çš„ SqlId + ç¼–å†™çš„ sql æŸ¥è¯¢è¯­å¥ + å‚æ•°
     * 2. ä¸æ•°æ®åº“åŒä¸€æ¬¡ä¼šè¯æœŸé—´æŸ¥è¯¢åˆ°çš„æ•°æ®ä¼šæ”¾åœ¨æœ¬åœ°ç¼“å­˜ä¸­
     * 3. ä»¥åå¦‚æœéœ€è¦è·å–ç›¸åŒçš„æ•°æ®ï¼Œç›´æ¥ä»ç¼“å­˜ä¸­æ‹¿ï¼Œæ²¡å¿…è¦å†å»æŸ¥è¯¢æ•°æ®åº“
     *
     * ä¸€çº§ç¼“å­˜å¤±æ•ˆæƒ…å†µï¼šï¼ˆæ²¡æœ‰ä½¿ç”¨åˆ°å½“å‰ä¸€çº§ç¼“å­˜çš„æƒ…å†µï¼Œéœ€è¦å‘æ•°æ®åº“é‡æ–°å‘é€æŸ¥è¯¢è¯­å¥ï¼‰
     * 1. sqlSessionä¸åŒ
     * 2. sqlSessionç›¸åŒï¼ŒæŸ¥è¯¢æ¡ä»¶ä¸åŒ
     * 3. sqlSessionç›¸åŒï¼Œä¸¤æ¬¡æŸ¥è¯¢ä¹‹é—´æ‰§è¡Œäº†å¢åˆ æ”¹æ“ä½œ
     * 4. sqlSessionç›¸åŒï¼Œæ‰‹åŠ¨æ¸…é™¤äº†ä¸€çº§ç¼“å­˜
     */
    @Test
    public void testFirstLevelCache() throws IOException {
        SqlSession sqlSession = getSqlSessionFactory().openSession(true);
        SqlSession sqlSession02 = getSqlSessionFactory().openSession(true);

        EmployeeCacheMapper mapper = sqlSession.getMapper(EmployeeCacheMapper.class);
        EmployeeCacheMapper mapper02 = sqlSession02.getMapper(EmployeeCacheMapper.class);
        Employee employee = mapper.selectEmployeeById(1);
        // mapper.insertEmployee(new Employee(null, "E_CC", null, null));
        sqlSession.clearCache();
        //Employee employee01 = mapper.selectEmployeeById(2);
        Employee employee01 = mapper.selectEmployeeById(1);
        System.out.println(employee == employee01);
        Employee employee02 = mapper02.selectEmployeeById(1);
        System.out.println(employee == employee02);
        sqlSession.close();
    }

    @Test
    public void testSecondLevelCache() throws IOException {
        SqlSessionFactory sqlSessionFactory = getSqlSessionFactory();
        SqlSessionFactory sqlSessionFactory02 = getSqlSessionFactory();
        System.out.println("SqlSessionFactory: " + 
                           (sqlSessionFactory == sqlSessionFactory02));//false
        // æ³¨æ„ï¼šå¿…é¡»æ˜¯åŒä¸€SqlSessionFactoryï¼Œå¦åˆ™ä¸ç”Ÿæ•ˆ
        SqlSession sqlSession = sqlSessionFactory.openSession(true);
        SqlSession sqlSession02 = sqlSessionFactory.openSession(true);
        EmployeeCacheMapper mapper = sqlSession.getMapper(EmployeeCacheMapper.class);
        EmployeeCacheMapper mapper02 = sqlSession02.getMapper(EmployeeCacheMapper.class);
        Employee employee = mapper.selectEmployeeById(1);
        sqlSession.close();
        Employee employee02 = mapper02.selectEmployeeById(1);
        System.out.println(employee);
        System.out.println(employee02);
        System.out.println("Employee: " + (employee02 == employee));
    }

                                                                                                                                                                                                                        EmployeeMapper

                                                                                                                                                                                                                        public interface EmployeeMapper {
    /**
     * æŸ¥è¯¢ EmployeeList
     * @return
     */
    public List<Employee> selectAllEmployee();
}

                                                                                                                                                                                                                        EmployeeService

                                                                                                                                                                                                                        public interface EmployeeService {

    List<Employee> getEmployeeList();
}

                                                                                                                                                                                                                        EmployeeServiceImpl

                                                                                                                                                                                                                        @Service
public class EmployeeServiceImpl implements EmployeeService {
    @Autowired
    private EmployeeMapper employeeMapper;

    @Autowired
    private SqlSession sqlSession;
    
    @Override
    public List<Employee> getEmployeeList() {
        // æ‰¹é‡æ‰§è¡Œ
        // EmployeeMapper mapper = sqlSession.getMapper(EmployeeMapper.class);
        return employeeMapper.selectAllEmployee();
    }
}

                                                                                                                                                                                                                        EmployeeController

                                                                                                                                                                                                                        @Controller
public class EmployeeController {
    @Autowired
    private EmployeeService employeeService;

    @GetMapping("/getEmployeeList")
    public String getEmployeeList(Map<String, Object> map) {
        map.put("employeeList", employeeService.getEmployeeList());
        return "list";
    }
}

                                                                                                                                                                                                                        MBGTest

                                                                                                                                                                                                                        public class MybatisTest {

    @Test
    public void testMBG() throws Exception {
        List<String> warnings = new ArrayList<String>();
        boolean overwrite = true;
        File configFile = new File("generatorConfig.xml");
        ConfigurationParser cp = new ConfigurationParser(warnings);
        Configuration config = cp.parseConfiguration(configFile);
        DefaultShellCallback callback = new DefaultShellCallback(overwrite);
        MyBatisGenerator myBatisGenerator = new MyBatisGenerator(config, callback, warnings);
        myBatisGenerator.generate(null);
    }
}

                                                                                                                                                                                                                        æµ‹è¯•ï¼š

                                                                                                                                                                                                                            public SqlSessionFactory getSqlSessionFactory() throws IOException {
        return new SqlSessionFactoryBuilder().build(Resources.getResourceAsStream("mybatis-config.xml"));
    }
    @Test
    public void testMybatis3Criteria() throws Exception {
        // æ–¹æ³•æŠ›å‡ºå¼‚å¸¸åï¼Œtryä¸éœ€è¦catch
        try (SqlSession sqlSession = getSqlSessionFactory().openSession()) {
            EmployeeMapper mapper = sqlSession.getMapper(EmployeeMapper.class);
            //æ¡ä»¶æŸ¥è¯¢
            EmployeeExample employeeExample = new EmployeeExample();
            EmployeeExample.Criteria criteria = employeeExample.createCriteria();
            criteria.andLastNameLike("%C%");
            
            List<Employee> employees = mapper.selectByExample(employeeExample);
            employees.forEach(System.out::println);
        }
    }
}

                                                                                                                                                                                                                        # Mybatis æ‰§è¡ŒåŸç†

                                                                                                                                                                                                                        # æ•´ä½“æ¶æ„

                                                                                                                                                                                                                        ç®€å•è¯´æ˜ï¼š

                                                                                                                                                                                                                        • Mybatis é…ç½® SqlMapConfig.xmlï¼Œæ­¤æ–‡ä»¶ä½œä¸º Mybatis çš„å…¨å±€é…ç½®æ–‡ä»¶ï¼Œé…ç½®äº† Mybatis çš„è¿è¡Œç¯å¢ƒç­‰ä¿¡æ¯ã€‚
                                                                                                                                                                                                                          mapper.xml æ–‡ä»¶å³ SQL æ˜ å°„æ–‡ä»¶ï¼Œæ–‡ä»¶ä¸­é…ç½®äº†æ“ä½œæ•°æ®åº“çš„ SQL è¯­å¥ã€‚æ­¤æ–‡ä»¶éœ€è¦åœ¨ SqlMapConfig.xml ä¸­åŠ è½½ã€‚
                                                                                                                                                                                                                        • é€šè¿‡ Mybatis ç¯å¢ƒç­‰é…ç½®ä¿¡æ¯æ„é€  SqlSessionFactory å³ä¼šè¯å·¥å‚ã€‚
                                                                                                                                                                                                                        • ç”±ä¼šè¯å·¥å‚åˆ›å»º sqlSession å³ä¼šè¯ï¼Œæ“ä½œæ•°æ®åº“éœ€è¦é€šè¿‡ sqlSession è¿›è¡Œã€‚
                                                                                                                                                                                                                        • Mybatis åº•å±‚è‡ªå®šä¹‰äº† Executor æ‰§è¡Œå™¨æ¥å£æ“ä½œæ•°æ®åº“ï¼ŒExecutor æ¥å£æœ‰ä¸¤ä¸ªå®ç°ï¼Œä¸€ä¸ªæ˜¯åŸºæœ¬æ‰§è¡Œå™¨ã€ä¸€ä¸ªæ˜¯ç¼“å­˜æ‰§è¡Œå™¨ã€‚

                                                                                                                                                                                                                        1. ç¼–å†™æ’ä»¶å®ç° Interceptor æ¥å£ï¼Œå¹¶ä½¿ç”¨ @Intercepts æ³¨è§£å®Œæˆæ’ä»¶ç­¾å

                                                                                                                                                                                                                          public interface Interceptor {

  Object intercept(Invocation invocation) throws Throwable;

  default Object plugin(Object target) {
    return Plugin.wrap(target, this);
  }

  default void setProperties(Properties properties) {
    // NOP
  }

}

@Intercepts({
        @Signature(type = StatementHandler.class,
                method = "parameterize", args = Statement.class)
})
public class CustomFirstPlugin implements Interceptor {

    /**
     * æ‹¦æˆªç›®æ ‡æ–¹æ³•æ‰§è¡Œ
     */
    @Override
    public Object intercept(Invocation invocation) throws Throwable {
        //æ’ä»¶æ‹¦æˆªçš„æ–¹æ³•
        System.out.println("Custom FirstPlugin intercept: " + invocation.getMethod());
        //æ‰§è¡Œç›®æ ‡æ–¹æ³•
        Object proceed = invocation.proceed();
        return proceed;
    }

    /**
     * ç”ŸæˆåŠ¨æ€ä»£ç†å¯¹è±¡ï¼Œå¯ä»¥ä½¿ç”¨ MyBatis æ
     * ä¾›çš„ Plugin ç±»çš„ wrapæ–¹æ³•

    @Override
    public Object plugin(Object target) {
        /*
            æ’ä»¶åŒ…è£…çš„æ–¹æ³•ï¼Œtargetï¼šè¦åŒ…è£…çš„å¯¹è±¡
         */
        System.out.println("Custom FirstPlugin plugin: " + target);
        //Mybatisæä¾›äº†Plugin.wrapä½¿ç”¨å½“å‰æ‹¦æˆªå™¨åŒ…è£…ç›®æ ‡æ–¹æ³•ï¼Œè¿”å›åŒ…è£…åçš„å¯¹è±¡
        Object wrap = Plugin.wrap(target, this);
        return wrap;
    }

    /**
     * æ³¨å…¥æ’ä»¶é…ç½®æ—¶è®¾ç½®çš„å±æ€§
     */
    @Override
    public void setProperties(Properties properties) {
        //Interceptor.super.setProperties(properties);
        System.out.println(properties);
    }
}

                                                                                                                                                                                                                        @Intercepts({
        @Signature(type = StatementHandler.class,
                method = "parameterize", args = Statement.class)
})
public class CustomParameterPlugin implements Interceptor {

    /**
     * æ‹¦æˆªç›®æ ‡æ–¹æ³•æ‰§è¡Œ
     */
    @Override
    public Object intercept(Invocation invocation) throws Throwable {
        //æ’ä»¶æ‹¦æˆªçš„æ–¹æ³•
        System.out.println("Custom SecondPlugin intercept: " + invocation.getMethod());
        Object target = invocation.getTarget();
        System.out.println("intercept: " + target);
        //è·å–targetçš„å…ƒæ•°æ®
        MetaObject metaObject = SystemMetaObject.forObject(target);
        Object objectValue = metaObject.getValue("parameterHandler.parameterObject");
        System.out.println("é¢„ç¼–è¯‘å‚æ•°ï¼š" + objectValue);
        //ä¿®æ”¹å‚æ•°
        metaObject.setValue("parameterHandler.parameterObject",2);
        //æ‰§è¡Œç›®æ ‡æ–¹æ³•
        Object proceed = invocation.proceed();
        return proceed;
    }

    /**
     * ç”ŸæˆåŠ¨æ€ä»£ç†å¯¹è±¡ï¼Œå¯ä»¥ä½¿ç”¨ MyBatis æ
     * ä¾›çš„ Plugin ç±»çš„ wrapæ–¹æ³•
     */
    @Override
    public Object plugin(Object target) {
        /*
            æ’ä»¶åŒ…è£…çš„æ–¹æ³•ï¼Œtargetï¼šè¦åŒ…è£…çš„å¯¹è±¡
         */
        System.out.println("Custom SecondPlugin plugin: " + target);
        //Mybatisæä¾›äº†Plugin.wrapä½¿ç”¨å½“å‰æ‹¦æˆªå™¨åŒ…è£…ç›®æ ‡æ–¹æ³•ï¼Œè¿”å›åŒ…è£…åçš„å¯¹è±¡
        Object wrap = Plugin.wrap(target, this);
        return wrap;
    }

    /**
     * æ³¨å…¥æ’ä»¶é…ç½®æ—¶è®¾ç½®çš„å±æ€§
     */
    @Override
    public void setProperties(Properties properties) {
        //Interceptor.super.setProperties(properties);
        System.out.println(properties);
    }
}

    </select>

                                                                                                                                                                                                                        æµ‹è¯•ï¼šï¼ˆMybatisPluginMapperTestï¼‰

                                                                                                                                                                                                                            /**
     * æµ‹è¯•åˆ†é¡µï¼š
     *      1. é…ç½®æ’ä»¶
     *      2. Page page = PageHelper.startPage(3, 5);
     */
    @Test
    public void testPlugin() throws IOException {
        SqlSessionFactory sqlSessionFactory = getSqlSessionFactory();
        try (SqlSession sqlSession = sqlSessionFactory.openSession()) {
            EmployeePageHelperMapper mapper = sqlSession.getMapper(EmployeePageHelperMapper.class);
            Page<Object> page = PageHelper.startPage(15, 2);
            List<Employee> employeeList = mapper.selectEmployeeList();
            employeeList.forEach(System.out::println);
            System.out.println("pageNum: " + page.getPageNum());
            System.out.println("pages: " + page.getPages());
            System.out.println("pageSize: " + page.getPageSize());
            System.out.println("total:" + page.getTotal());
            //åŠŸèƒ½æ›´å¤šçš„ PageInfo
            PageInfo<Employee> pageInfo = new PageInfo<>(employeeList);
            System.out.println("hasPreviousPage: " + pageInfo.isHasPreviousPage());
            System.out.println("hasNextPage: " + pageInfo.isHasNextPage());
            System.out.println("firstPage: " + pageInfo.isIsFirstPage());
            System.out.println("lastPage: " + pageInfo.isIsLastPage());

            //ä¼ å…¥å‚æ•°ï¼Œè¿ç»­æ˜¾ç¤ºå¤šå°‘é¡µ
            PageInfo<Employee> employeePageInfo = new PageInfo<>(employeeList,5);
            int[] navigatePageNums = employeePageInfo.getNavigatepageNums();
            System.out.println(Arrays.toString(navigatePageNums));
        }
    }

                                                                                                                                                                                                                        Configures the default executor. SIMPLE executor does nothing special. REUSE executor reuses prepared statements. BATCH executor reuses statements and batches updates.
OPTIONS: SIMPLE REUSE BATCH
DEFAULT: SIMPLE

                                                                                                                                                                                                                        MybatisBatchMapperTest

                                                                                                                                                                                                                        public class MybatisBatchMapperTest {
    public SqlSessionFactory getSqlSessionFactory() throws IOException {
        return new SqlSessionFactoryBuilder()
                .build(Resources.getResourceAsStream("mybatis-config.xml"));
    }

    /**
     * æ‰¹é‡æ’å…¥ï¼šæ³¨æ„è°ƒç”¨çš„ä»æ˜¯æ’å…¥å•ä¸ªå¯¹è±¡çš„æ–¹æ³•
     */
    @Test
    public void testBatchMapper() throws IOException {
        SqlSessionFactory sqlSessionFactory = getSqlSessionFactory();
        SqlSession sqlSession = sqlSessionFactory.openSession(ExecutorType.BATCH);
        EmployeeBatchMapper mapper = sqlSession.getMapper(EmployeeBatchMapper.class);
        for (int i = 0; i < 5; i++) {
            Employee employee = new Employee(
                    UUID.randomUUID().toString().substring(0, 6), 
                    "M", 
                    "mineting@example");
            mapper.batchInsertEmployee(employee);
        }
        sqlSession.commit();
        sqlSession.close();
    }

}

                                                                                                                                                                                                                        # å­˜å‚¨è¿‡ç¨‹ï¼ˆæœ‰BUGï¼‰

                                                                                                                                                                                                                        å­˜å‚¨è¿‡ç¨‹ä¸€èˆ¬ç”¨äºå°è£…è¾ƒä¸ºå¤æ‚çš„ SQL è¯­å¥ï¼Œç”¨äºæ•°æ®åº“è¿›è¡Œé¢„ç¼–è¯‘ã€‚

                                                                                                                                                                                                                        ä»¥ Oracle çš„åˆ†é¡µä¸ºä¾‹ï¼ŒOracle é€šè¿‡ rownum å®ç°åˆ†é¡µï¼Œrownum ä½œä¸ºä¼ªåˆ—ï¼Œæ˜¯å…ˆæ ¹æ® where æ¡ä»¶æŸ¥å‡ºæ•°æ®ï¼Œä¹‹åæ‰ä¼šå¯¹ rownum åˆ†é…æ•°æ®ï¼Œå› æ­¤ rownum >= 3 and rownum <=5 è¿™ç§æ–¹å¼æ˜¯æŸ¥ä¸åˆ°æ•°æ®çš„ï¼Œå³éœ€è¦é€šè¿‡å­æŸ¥è¯¢ç»™ rownum ä¸€ä¸ªåˆ«åï¼Œåœ¨æ­¤åŸºç¡€ä¸Šè¿›è¡Œåˆ†é¡µï¼Œå¯ä»¥å…ˆå¾—åˆ° rownum <=5 å†å¾—åˆ° rownum >= 1

                                                                                                                                                                                                                        åˆ†é¡µç¤ºä¾‹ï¼š

                                                                                                                                                                                                                        -- åˆ†é¡µï¼šå­˜å‚¨è¿‡ç¨‹
create or replace procedure 
       get_page(
          p_start in int,p_end in int,p_count out int,p_emps out sys_refcursor
       )
       begin 
         select count(*) into p_count from emp;
         open p_emps for
              select * from (select rownum rn,e.* from emp e where rownum<=p_end) 
              where rn >= p_start;
       end to_page;

-- æŸ¥è¯¢åˆ›å»ºçš„å­˜å‚¨è¿‡ç¨‹
select * from user_source;

-- æµ‹è¯•è°ƒç”¨å­˜å‚¨è¿‡ç¨‹

                                                                                                                                                                                                                        MyBatis è°ƒç”¨å­˜å‚¨è¿‡ç¨‹ï¼š

                                                                                                                                                                                                                        åˆ›å»ºåˆ†é¡µå¯¹è±¡ OraclePageï¼š

                                                                                                                                                                                                                        /**
 * å°è£… Oracle åˆ†é¡µæŸ¥è¯¢æ•°æ®
 */
@Data
@AllArgsConstructor
@NoArgsConstructor
public class OraclePage implements Serializable {

    private int start;
    private int end;
    private int count;
    private List<Employee> employeeList;

    public OraclePage(int start, int end) {
        this.start = start;
        this.end = end;
    }
}

                                                                                                                                                                                                                        EmployeeProcedureMapper.xml

                                                                                                                                                                                                                        <?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8" ?>
<!DOCTYPE mapper
        PUBLIC "-//mybatis.org//DTD Mapper 3.0//EN"
        "http://mybatis.org/dtd/mybatis-3-mapper.dtd">
<mapper namespace="com.example.mybatis.mapper.EmployeeProcedureMapper">

    <!--
        1. ä½¿ç”¨ select æ ‡ç­¾å®šä¹‰è°ƒç”¨å­˜å‚¨è¿‡ç¨‹
	    2. statementType="CALLABLE":è°ƒç”¨å­˜å‚¨è¿‡ç¨‹
	    3. {call procedure_name(params)}
    -->
    <select id="getOraclePageByProcedure" statementType="CALLABLE" databaseId="oracle">
        {call proc_pagehelper(
            #{start,mode=IN,jdbcType=INTEGER},
            #{end,mode=IN,jdbcType=INTEGER},
            #{count,mode=OUT,jdbcType=INTEGER},
            #{emps,mode=OUT,jdbcType=CURSOR,javaType=ResultSet,resultMap=employeePageMap}
        )}
    </select>

    <resultMap id="employeePageMap" type="com.example.mybatis.bean.Employee">
        <id column="empno" property="id"/>
        <result column="ename" property="lastName"/>
    </resultMap>
    
</mapper>

                                                                                                                                                                                                                        æµ‹è¯•ï¼šMybatisProcedureMapperTest

                                                                                                                                                                                                                        public class MybatisProcedureMapperTest {
    public SqlSessionFactory getSqlSessionFactory() throws IOException {
        return new SqlSessionFactoryBuilder()
                .build(Resources.getResourceAsStream("mybatis-config.xml"));
    }

    /**
     * å­˜å‚¨è¿‡ç¨‹
     */
    @Test
    public void testBatchMapper() throws IOException {
        SqlSessionFactory sqlSessionFactory = getSqlSessionFactory();
        SqlSession sqlSession = sqlSessionFactory.openSession();
        EmployeeProcedureMapper mapper = sqlSession.getMapper(EmployeeProcedureMapper.class);
        OraclePage page = new OraclePage(2, 5);
        mapper.getOraclePageByProcedure(page);
        List<Employee> employeeList = page.getEmployeeList();
        employeeList.forEach(System.out::println);
        sqlSession.close();
    }

}

                                                                                                                                                                                                                        # ç±»å‹å¤„ç†å™¨

                                                                                                                                                                                                                        public interface TypeHandler<T> {

  void setParameter(PreparedStatement ps, int i, T parameter, JdbcType jdbcType) throws SQLException;
  // é€šè¿‡åˆ—åè·å–å€¼  
  T getResult(ResultSet rs, String columnName) throws SQLException;
  // é€šè¿‡åˆ—çš„ç´¢å¼•è·å–å€¼
  T getResult(ResultSet rs, int columnIndex) throws SQLException;

  T getResult(CallableStatement cs, int columnIndex) throws SQLException;

}

                                                                                                                                                                                                                        # è‡ªå®šä¹‰ TypeHandler å¤„ç†æšä¸¾

                                                                                                                                                                                                                        alter table tbl_employee add employeeStatus varchar(11);

                                                                                                                                                                                                                        Employee

                                                                                                                                                                                                                        @Data
@AllArgsConstructor
@NoArgsConstructor
public class Employee implements Serializable {
    private Integer id;
    private String lastName;
    private String gender;
    private String email;

    private EmployeeStatus status;

    public Employee(String lastName, String gender, String email) {
        this.lastName = lastName;
        this.gender = gender;
        this.email = email;
    }

    public Employee(String lastName, String gender, String email, EmployeeStatus status) {
        this.lastName = lastName;
        this.gender = gender;
        this.email = email;
        this.status = status;
    }
}

                                                                                                                                                                                                                        EmployeeStatus

                                                                                                                                                                                                                        public enum EmployeeStatus {
    LOGIN(100,"ç™»å½•"),LOGOUT(200,"é€€å‡º"),REMOVE(300,"åˆ é™¤");

    private Integer code;
    private String message;

    private EmployeeStatus(Integer code, String message){
        this.code = code;
        this.message = message;
    }
    public static EmployeeStatus getEmpStatusByCode(Integer code) {
        switch (code) {
            case 100:
                return LOGIN;
            case 200:
                return LOGOUT;
            default:
                return REMOVE;
        }
    }
}

                                                                                                                                                                                                                        è‡ªå®šä¹‰ç±»å‹å¤„ç†å™¨

                                                                                                                                                                                                                        package com.example.mybatis.typehandlers;

import com.example.mybatis.bean.EmployeeStatus;
import org.apache.ibatis.type.JdbcType;
import org.apache.ibatis.type.TypeHandler;

import java.sql.CallableStatement;
import java.sql.PreparedStatement;
import java.sql.ResultSet;
import java.sql.SQLException;

/**
 * è‡ªå®šä¹‰ç±»å‹å¤„ç†å™¨
 */
public class EmployeeEnumTypeHandler implements TypeHandler<EmployeeStatus> {

    @Override
    public void setParameter(PreparedStatement ps, int i, EmployeeStatus parameter, JdbcType jdbcType) throws SQLException {
        ps.setString(i, parameter.getCode().toString());
    }

    @Override
    public EmployeeStatus getResult(ResultSet rs, String columnName) throws SQLException {
        return EmployeeStatus.getEmployeeStatusByCode(rs.getInt(columnName));
    }

    @Override
    public EmployeeStatus getResult(ResultSet rs, int columnIndex) throws SQLException {
        return EmployeeStatus.getEmployeeStatusByCode(rs.getInt(columnIndex));
    }

    @Override
    public EmployeeStatus getResult(CallableStatement cs, int columnIndex) throws SQLException {
        return null;
    }
}

                                                                                                                                                                                                                        å…¨å±€é…ç½®ï¼ŒæŒ‡å®šå¯¹å“ªä¸€ä¸ªç±»åº”ç”¨è¯¥è§„åˆ™

                                                                                                                                                                                                                        <!--
    ç±»å‹å¤„ç†å™¨:
    1. å…¨å±€å¤„ç†å™¨

                 javaType="com.example.mybatis.bean.EmpStatus"/>
     2. å±€éƒ¨å¤„ç†ï¼š
        æ’å…¥æ—¶ï¼šinsert into tbl_employee(last_name, gender, email, emp_status)
                values (#{lastName}, #{gender}, #{email}, #{empStatus,typeHandler=....})
        æŸ¥è¯¢æ—¶ï¼šåœ¨ResultMapä¸­å®šä¹‰
               <result column="emp_status" property="empStatus" typeHandler=""/>
-->

                     javaType="com.example.mybatis.bean.EmployeeStatus"/>

                                                                                                                                                                                                                        EmployeeTypeHandlerMapper.xml

                                                                                                                                                                                                                        <?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8" ?>
<!DOCTYPE mapper
        PUBLIC "-//mybatis.org//DTD Mapper 3.0//EN"
        "http://mybatis.org/dtd/mybatis-3-mapper.dtd">
<mapper namespace="com.example.mybatis.mapper.EmployeeTypeHandlerMapper">

    <resultMap id="BaseResultMap" type="com.example.mybatis.bean.Employee">
        <id column="id" property="id"/>
        <result column="last_name" property="lastName"/>
        <result column="employeeStatus" property="employeeStatus"/>
    </resultMap>

    <insert id="insertEmployee" useGeneratedKeys="true" keyProperty="id">
        insert into tbl_employee(last_name, gender, email, employeeStatus)
        values (#{lastName}, #{gender}, #{email}, #{employeeStatus})
    </insert>

    <select id="selectEmployeeById" resultMap="BaseResultMap">
        select * from tbl_employee where id = #{id}
    </select>

</mapper>

                                                                                                                                                                                                                        æµ‹è¯• MybatisTypeHandlerMapperTestï¼š

                                                                                                                                                                                                                        public class MybatisTypeHandlerMapperTest {
    public SqlSessionFactory getSqlSessionFactory() throws IOException {
        return new SqlSessionFactoryBuilder()
                .build(Resources.getResourceAsStream("mybatis-config.xml"));
    }

    /**
     * è‡ªå®šä¹‰ç±»å‹å¤„ç†å™¨
     */
    @Test
    public void testBatchMapper() throws IOException {
        SqlSessionFactory sqlSessionFactory = getSqlSessionFactory();
        SqlSession sqlSession = sqlSessionFactory.openSession();
        try {
            EmployeeTypeHandlerMapper mapper =
                    sqlSession.getMapper(EmployeeTypeHandlerMapper.class);
            Employee employee = new Employee("enum", "M", "enum@example.com", EmployeeStatus.LOGOUT);
            mapper.insertEmployee(employee);
            System.out.println(employee.getId() + " : " + employee.getEmployeeStatus());
            System.out.println(mapper.selectEmployeeById(16));
            sqlSession.commit();
        } finally {
            sqlSession.close();
        }
    }
}
